   164→  if (!/^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+$/.test(agentId)) {

   168→  // Check cache first  
   169→  const cached = reachableCache.get(agentId)  
   170→  if (cached && Date.now() < cached.expiresAt) {  
   171→    return { data: { reachableAgentIds: cached.ids }, status: 200 }  
   172→  }

   175→  const reachableAgentIds: string[] = []  
   176→  
   177→  for (const agent of allAgents) {  
   178→    if (agent.id === agentId) continue

   180→  
   181→    const result = checkMessageAllowed({  
   182→      senderAgentId: agentId,  
   183→      recipientAgentId: agent.id,  
   184→    })  
   185→  
   186→    if (result.allowed) {  
   187→      reachableAgentIds.push(agent.id)  
   188→    }  
   189→  }  
   190→  
   191→  reachableCache.set(agentId, { ids: reachableAgentIds, expiresAt: Date.now() + CACHE_TTL_MS })

   193→  // Evict stale entries  
   194→  const now = Date.now()  
   195→  for (const [key, entry] of reachableCache) {  
   196→    if (now >= entry.expiresAt) reachableCache.delete(key)

   199→  
   200→function ensureTeamsDir() {  
   201→  if (!fs.existsSync(TEAMS_DIR)) {  
   202→    fs.mkdirSync(TEAMS_DIR, { recursive: true })  
   203→  }  
   204→}  
   205→  
   206→export function loadTeams(): Team[] {  
   207→  try {  
   208→    ensureTeamsDir()  
   209→    if (!fs.existsSync(TEAMS_FILE)) {  
   210→      return []  
   211→    }  
   212→    const data = fs.readFileSync(TEAMS_FILE, 'utf-8')  
   213→    const parsed: TeamsFile = JSON.parse(data)  
   214→    const teams = Array.isArray(parsed.teams) ? parsed.teams : []  
   215→  
   216→    // Idempotent convergent migration: ensure all teams have a type field (default to 'open').  
   217→    // If two concurrent calls both trigger the migration, both produce the same result  
   218→    // (every team without a type gets 'open'), so the last write wins safely.  
   219→    // The migrationDone flag ensures we only persist the migration once per process.  
   220→    let needsSave = false  
   221→    for (const team of teams) {  
   222→      if (!team.type) {  
   223→        team.type = 'open'  
   224→        needsSave = true  
   225→      }  
   226→    }  
   227→    // CC-003: Migration write is idempotent and safe without lock — worst case is a redundant write.  
   228→    // When called from getTeam() (no lock), two concurrent migrations may both write, but produce identical output.  
   229→    if (needsSave && !migrationDone) {  
   230→      migrationDone = true  
   231→      saveTeams(teams)  
   232→    }  
   233→  
   234→    return teams  
   235→  } catch (error) {  
   236→    console.error('Failed to load teams:', error)  
   237→    return []  
   238→  }  
   239→}  
   240→  
   241→export function saveTeams(teams: Team[]): boolean {  
   242→  try {  
   243→    ensureTeamsDir()  
   244→    const file: TeamsFile = { version: 1, teams }  
   245→    // Atomic write: write to temp file then rename to avoid corruption on crash  
   246→    const tmpFile = TEAMS_FILE + '.tmp'  
   247→    fs.writeFileSync(tmpFile, JSON.stringify(file, null, 2), 'utf-8')

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * File Lock — in-process mutex for serializing load→modify→save operations  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Prevents concurrent read-modify-write races within a single Node.js process.  
     5→ * Each registry file gets its own named lock. When one API request is mid-write,  
     6→ * other requests for the same file queue up and run sequentially.  
     7→ *  
     8→ * This is sufficient for Phase 1 (single Next.js process, localhost).  
     9→ * For multi-process deployments, replace with advisory file locks (e.g., proper-lockfile).  
    10→ */  
    11→  
    12→/**  
    13→ * LOCK ORDERING INVARIANT:  
    14→ * When acquiring multiple locks, always acquire in this order:  
    15→ *   1. 'teams'  
    16→ *   2. 'transfers'  
    17→ *   3. 'governance'  
    18→ * Violating this order will cause deadlock.  
    19→ *  
    20→ * Current nested lock usage:  
    21→ * - transfers/[id]/resolve/route.ts: acquires 'teams' then 'transfers' (via resolveTransferRequest)  
    22→ */  
    23→  
    24→// Map of lock name -> queue of pending resolve callbacks  
    25→const locks = new Map<string, Array<() => void>>()  
    26→// Set of currently held lock names  
    27→const held = new Set<string>()  
    28→  
    29→/**  
    30→ * Acquire a named lock. Returns a release function.  
    31→ * If the lock is already held, the caller awaits until it is released.  
    32→ */  
    33→export function acquireLock(name: string): Promise<() => void> {  
    34→  if (!held.has(name)) {  
    35→    // Lock is free — acquire immediately  
    36→    held.add(name)  
    37→    return Promise.resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    38→  }  
    39→  
    40→  // Lock is held — enqueue and wait  
    41→  return new Promise<() => void>((resolve) => {  
    42→    if (!locks.has(name)) {  
    43→      locks.set(name, [])  
    44→    }  
    45→    locks.get(name)!.push(() => {  
    46→      resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    47→    })  
    48→  })  
    49→}  
    50→  
    51→/**  
    52→ * Release a named lock and wake the next waiter if any.  
    

... [1042 more chars truncated]  

</details>

   131→export async function createNewTeam(params: CreateTeamParams): Promise<ServiceResult<{ team: any }>> {  
   132→  const { name, description, agentIds } = params  
   133→  
   134→  if (!name || typeof name !== 'string') {  
   135→    return { error: 'Team name is required', status: 400 }  
   136→  }  
   137→  
   138→  if (agentIds && !Array.isArray(agentIds)) {  
   139→    return { error: 'agentIds must be an array', status: 400 }  
   140→  }  
   141→  
   142→  // Governance: validate type field  
   143→  if (params.type && params.type !== 'open' && params.type !== 'closed') {  
   144→    return { error: 'type must be "open" or "closed"', status: 400 }  
   145→  }  
   146→  
   147→  try {  
   148→    // Pass governance context (managerId + agent names for collision checks) to createTeam  
   149→    const managerId = getManagerId()  
   150→    const agentNames = loadAgents().map(a => a.name).filter(Boolean)  
   151→    const team = await createTeam(  
   152→      { name, description, agentIds: agentIds || [], type: params.type, chiefOfStaffId: params.chiefOfStaffId },  
   153→      managerId,  
   154→      agentNames  
   155→    )  
   156→    return { data: { team }, status: 201 }  
   157→  } catch (error) {  
   158→    // TeamValidationException carries a specific HTTP status code from governance rules  
   159→    if (error instanceof TeamValidationException) {  
   160→      return { error: error.message, status: error.code }  
   161→    }  
   162→    console.error('Failed to create team:', error)  
   163→    return { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to create team', status: 500 }  
   164→  }  
   165→}

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { verifyPassword, loadGovernance, getManagerId } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→import { getTeam, updateTeam, TeamValidationException } from '@/lib/team-registry'  
     4→import { getAgent } from '@/lib/agent-registry'  
     5→import { checkRateLimit, recordFailure, resetRateLimit } from '@/lib/rate-limit'  
     6→import { isValidUuid } from '@/lib/validation'  
     7→  
     8→export async function POST(  
     9→  request: NextRequest,  
    10→  { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> }  
    11→) {  
    12→  try {  
    13→    const { id } = await params  
    14→    if (!isValidUuid(id)) {  
    15→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid team ID format' }, { status: 400 })  
    16→    }  
    17→    let body  
    18→    try { body = await request.json() } catch { return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' }, { status: 400 }) }  
    19→    const { agentId: cosAgentId, password } = body  
    20→  
    21→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string') {  
    22→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    23→    }  
    24→  
    25→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    26→    if (!config.passwordHash) {  
    27→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password not set' }, { status: 400 })  
    28→    }  
    29→  
    30→    // Rate limit password verification to prevent brute-force attacks  
    31→    const rateCheck = checkRateLimit('governance-cos-auth')  
    32→    if (!rateCheck.allowed) {  
    33→      return NextResponse.json(  
    34→        { error: `Too many failed password attempts. Try again in ${Math.ceil(rateCheck.retryAfterMs / 1000)}s` },  
    35→        { status: 429 }  
    36→      )  
    37→    }  
    38→

    42→  if (input.requestingAgentId === undefined) {  
    43→    return { allowed: true }

   139→export function updateTask(  
   140→  teamId: string,  
   141→  taskId: string,  
   142→  updates: Partial<Pick<Task, 'subject' | 'description' | 'status' | 'assigneeAgentId' | 'blockedBy' | 'priority'>>

    92→export function updateDocument(  
    93→  teamId: string,  
    94→  docId: string,  
    95→  updates: Partial<Pick<TeamDocument, 'title' | 'content' | 'pinned' | 'tags'>>  
    96→): Promise<TeamDocument | null> {  
    97→  return withLock('documents-' + teamId, () => {  
    98→    const documents = loadDocuments(teamId)  
    99→    const index = documents.findIndex(d => d.id === docId)  
   100→    if (index === -1) return null  
   101→  
   102→    documents[index] = {  
   103→      ...documents[index],  
   104→      ...updates,  
   105→      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),  
   106→    }  
   107→  
   108→    saveDocuments(teamId, documents)  
   109→    return documents[index]  
   110→  })  
   111→}  
   112→  
   113→export function deleteDocument(teamId: string, docId: string): Promise<boolean> {  
   114→  return withLock('documents-' + teamId, () => {  
   115→    const documents = loadDocuments(teamId)  
   116→    const filtered = documents.filter(d => d.id !== docId)  
   117→    if (filtered.length === documents.length) return false  
   118→    saveDocuments(teamId, filtered)  
   119→    return true  
   120→  })  
   121→}

     1→import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach } from 'vitest'  
     2→  
     3→// Note: team-api tests mock 'fs' directly at the module level below, not via  
     4→// team-registry — the fs mock intercepts all filesystem calls from any module  
     5→// (including team-registry) that the route handlers import.  
     6→  
     7→// ============================================================================  
     8→// Mocks  
     9→// ============================================================================  
    10→  
    11→let fsStore: Record<string, string> = {}  
    12→  
    13→vi.mock('fs', () => ({  
    14→  default: {  
    15→    existsSync: vi.fn((filePath: string) => filePath in fsStore),  
    16→    mkdirSync: vi.fn(),  
    17→    readFileSync: vi.fn((filePath: string) => {  
    18→      if (filePath in fsStore) return fsStore[filePath]  
    19→      throw new Error(`ENOENT: no such file or directory, open '${filePath}'`)  
    20→    }),  
    21→    writeFileSync: vi.fn((filePath: string, data: string) => {  
    22→      fsStore[filePath] = data  
    23→    }),  
    24→    renameSync: vi.fn((oldPath: string, newPath: string) => {

   200	function ensureTeamsDir() {  
   201	  if (!fs.existsSync(TEAMS_DIR)) {  
   202	    fs.mkdirSync(TEAMS_DIR, { recursive: true })  
   203	  }  
   204	}  
   205	  
   206	export function loadTeams(): Team[] {  
   207	  try {  
   208	    ensureTeamsDir()  
   209	    if (!fs.existsSync(TEAMS_FILE)) {  
   210	      return []  
   211	    }  
   212	    const data = fs.readFileSync(TEAMS_FILE, 'utf-8')  
   213	    const parsed: TeamsFile = JSON.parse(data)  
   214	    const teams = Array.isArray(parsed.teams) ? parsed.teams : []  
   215	  
   216	    // Idempotent convergent migration: ensure all teams have a type field (default to 'open').  
   217	    // If two concurrent calls both trigger the migration, both produce the same result  
   218	    // (every team without a type gets 'open'), so the last write wins safely.  
   219	    // The migrationDone flag ensures we only persist the migration once per process.  
   220	    let needsSave = false  
   221	    for (const team of teams) {  
   222	      if (!team.type) {  
   223	        team.type = 'open'  
   224	        needsSave = true  
   225	      }  
   226	    }  
   227	    // CC-003: Migration write is idempotent and safe without lock — worst case is a redundant write.  
   228	    // When called from getTeam() (no lock), two concurrent migrations may both write, but produce identical output.  
   229	    if (needsSave && !migrationDone) {  
   230	      migrationDone = true  
   231	      saveTeams(teams)  
   232	    }  
   233	  
   234	    return teams  
   235	  } catch (error) {  
   236	    console.error('Failed to load teams:', error)  
   237	    return []  
   238	  }  
   239	}  
   240

   247	    fs.writeFileSync(tmpFile, JSON.stringify(fil

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * Agent Authentication for Internal APIs  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Bridges AMP API key auth to governance-restricted internal API calls.  
     5→ * Agents must prove identity via Bearer token for operations requiring agent identity.  
     6→ *  
     7→ * Three outcomes:  
     8→ * 1. No auth headers → system owner (web UI) → { agentId: undefined }  
     9→ * 2. Valid Authorization: Bearer → authenticated agent → { agentId: 'uuid' }  
    10→ * 3. X-Agent-Id without valid Bearer, or invalid Bearer → { error, status: 401 }  
    11→ */  
    12→import { authenticateRequest } from './amp-auth'  
    13→  
    14→export interface AgentAuthResult {  
    15→  /** Verified agent ID, or undefined for system owner / web UI */  
    16→  agentId?: string  
    17→  /** Error message if authentication failed */  
    18→  error?: string  
    19→  /** HTTP status code for the error */  
    20→  status?: number  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→/**  
    24→ * Authenticate an agent from HTTP header values.  
    25→ *  
    26→ * @param authHeader - Value of Authorization header (or null)  
    27→ * @param agentIdHeader - Value of X-Agent-Id header (or null)  
    28→ * @returns AgentAuthResult with agentId for success, error for failure, or empty for system owner  
    29→ */  
    30→export function authenticateAgent(authHeader: string | null, agentIdHeader: string | null): AgentAuthResult {  
    31→  // Case 1: No auth attempt at all → system owner / web UI  
    32→  if (!authHeader && !agentIdHeader) {  
    33→    return {}  
    34→  }  
    35→  
    36→  // Case 2: X-Agent-Id present without Authorization → reject (identity spoofing)  
    37→  if (agentIdHeader && !authHeader) {  
    38→    return {  
    39→      error: 'Agent identity requires authentication. Include Authorization: Bearer <api-key> header.',  
    40→      status: 401  
    41→    }  
    42→  }  
    43→  
    44→  // Case 3: Authorization header present → validate API key  
    45→  if (authHeader) {  
    46→    const result = authenticateRequest(authHeader)  
 

... [715 more chars truncated]

    34→ * but adapted for display names (allows spaces, mixed case).  
    35→ */  
    36→export function sanitizeTeamName(raw: string): string {  
    37→  return raw  
    38→    .replace(/[\x00-\x1F\x7F]/g, '')  // Strip control characters (same as agent name sanitization)  
    39→    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')              // Collapse all whitespace into single space  
    40→    .trim()  
    41→}

**Result:**

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { checkMessageAllowed } from '@/lib/message-filter'  
     3→import { loadAgents } from '@/lib/agent-registry'  
     4→  
     5→// In-memory cache: avoids re-reading governance + teams files for every agent  
     6→// on each request. TTL of 5 seconds balances freshness with performance.  
     7→// Note: Cache does not auto-invalidate when governance/team config changes.  
     8→// TTL-based expiry handles staleness. Phase 2: add event-driven invalidation.  
     9→const cache = new Map<string, { ids: string[]; expiresAt: number }>()  
    10→const CACHE_TTL_MS = 5_000  
    11→  
    12→export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {  
    13→  try {  
    14→    const agentId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('agentId')  
    15→  
    16→    if (!agentId) {  
    17→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId query parameter is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    18→    }  
    19→  
    20→    if (!/^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+$/.test(agentId)) {  
    21→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid agentId format' }, { status: 400 })  
    22→    }  
    23→  
    24→    // Check cache first  
    25→    const cached = cache.get(agentId)  
    26→    if (cached && Date.now() < cached.expiresAt) {  
    27→      return NextResponse.json({ reachableAgentIds: cached.ids })  
    28→    }  
    29→  
    30→    // Cache miss or expired — compute reachable agents  
    31→    const allAgents = loadAgents()  
    32→    const reachableAgentIds: string[] = []  
    33→  
    34→    for (const agent of allAgents) {  
    35→      if (agent.id === agentId) continue  
    36→      if (agent.deletedAt) continue  
    37→  
    38→      const result = checkMessageAllowed({  
    39→        senderAgentId: agentId,  
    40→        recipientAgentId: agent.id,  
    41→      })  
    42→  
    43→      if (result.allowed) {  
    44→        reachableAgentIds.push(agent.id)  
    45→      }

<summary>🔧 Tool: Read -- `agent-auth.ts`</summary>

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * Agent Authentication for Internal APIs  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Bridges AMP API key auth to governance-restricted internal API calls.  
     5→ * Agents must prove identity via Bearer token for operations requiring agent identity.  
     6→ *  
     7→ * Three outcomes:  
     8→ * 1. No auth headers → system owner (web UI) → { agentId: undefined }  
     9→ * 2. Valid Authorization: Bearer → authenticated agent → { agentId: 'uuid' }  
    10→ * 3. X-Agent-Id without valid Bearer, or invalid Bearer → { error, status: 401 }  
    11→ */  
    12→import { authenticateRequest } from './amp-auth'  
    13→  
    14→export interface AgentAuthResult {  
    15→  /** Verified agent ID, or undefined for system owner / web UI */  
    16→  agentId?: string  
    17→  /** Error message if authentication failed */  
    18→  error?: string  
    19→  /** HTTP status code for the error */  
    20→  status?: number  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→/**  
    24→ * Authenticate an agent from HTTP header values.  
    25→ *  
    26→ * @param authHeader - Value of Authorization header (or null)  
    27→ * @param agentIdHeader - Value of X-Agent-Id header (or null)  
    28→ * @returns AgentAuthResult with agentId for success, error for failure, or empty for system owner  
    29→ */  
    30→export function authenticateAgent(authHeader: string | null, agentIdHeader: string | null): AgentAuthResult {  
    31→  // Case 1: No auth attempt at all → system owner / web UI  
    32→  if (!authHeader && !agentIdHeader) {  
    33→    return {}  
    34→  }  
    35→  
    36→  // Case 2: X-Agent-Id present without Authorization → reject (identity spoofing)  
    37→  if (agentIdHeader && !authHeader) {  
    38→    return {  
    39→      error: 'Agent identity requires authentication. Include Authorization: Bearer <api-key> header.',  
    40→      status: 401  
    41→    }  
    42→  }  
    43→  
    44→  // Case 3: Authorization header present → validate API key  
    45→  if (authHeader) {  
    46→    const result = authenticateRequest(authHeader)  
 

... [715 more chars truncated]  

</details>

   131→export async function createNewTeam(params: CreateTeamParams): Promise<ServiceResult<{ team: any }>> {  
   132→  const { name, description, agentIds } = params  
   133→

   135→    return { error: 'Team name is required', status: 400 }

   155→    )

   158→    // TeamValidationException carries a specific HTTP status code from governance rules

   160→      return { error: error.message, status: error.code }

   162→    console.error('Failed to create team:', error)

   197→export async function updateTeamById(id: string, params: UpdateTeamParams): Promise<ServiceResult<{ team: any }>> {

   304→export async function createTeamTask(teamId: string, params: CreateTaskParams): Promise<ServiceResult<{ task: any }>> {  
   305→  const team = getTeam(teamId)  
   306→  if (!team) {  
   307→    return { error: 'Team not found', status: 404 }  
   308→  }  
   309→  
   310→  // Governance ACL: closed teams restrict mutations to manager, COS, and members  
   311→  // Always call checkTeamAccess -- it handles undefined requestingAgentId (returns allowed: true)  
   312→  const { requestingAgentId, ...taskFields } = params  
   313→  const access = checkTeamAccess({ teamId, requestingAgentId })  
   314→  if (!access.allowed) {  
   315→    return { error: access.reason || 'Access denied', status: 403 }  
   316→  }  
   317→  
   318→  const { subject, description, assigneeAgentId, blockedBy, priority } = taskFields  
   319→  
   320→  if (!subject || typeof subject !== 'string' || !subject.trim()) {  
   321→    return { error: 'Subject is required', status: 400 }  
   322→  }  
   323→  
   324→  // Validate blockedBy is an array of strings if provided  
   325→  if (blockedBy !== undefined) {  
   326→    if (!Array.isArray(blockedBy) || !blockedBy.every((id: unknown) => typeof id === 'string')) {  
   327→      return { error: 'blockedBy must be an array of task ID strings', status: 400 }  
   328→    }  
   329→  }  
   330→  
   331→  try {

    17→    const agentId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('agentId')  
    18→    const status = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('status') // 'pending', 'approved', 'rejected', or null for all  
    19→  
    20→    if (status && !['pending','approved','rejected'].includes(status)) {  
    21→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid status filter' }, { status: 400 })  
    22→    }  
    23→  
    24→    let requests = loadTransfers()  
    25→  
    26→    if (teamId) {  
    27→      requests = requests.filter(r => r.fromTeamId === teamId || r.toTeamId === teamId)  
    28→    }  
    29→    if (agentId) {  
    30→      requests = requests.filter(r => r.agentId === agentId)  
    31→    }  
    32→    if (status) {  
    33→      requests = requests.filter(r => r.status === status)  
    34→    }  
    35→  
    36→    return NextResponse.json({ requests })  
    37→  } catch (error) {  
    38→    console.error('Error loading transfers:', error)  
    39→    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 })  
    40→  }  
    41→}

     1→/**  
     2→ * Agent Authentication for Internal APIs  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Bridges AMP API key auth to governance-restricted internal API calls.  
     5→ * Agents must prove identity via Bearer token for operations requiring agent identity.  
     6→ *

    19→  /** HTTP status code for the error */

    21→}

    23→/**

    40→      status: 401  
    41→    }  
    42→  }

     1→/**  
     2→ * Simple in-memory rate limiter for governance password operations.  
     3→ * Tracks failed attempts per key with a fixed time window.  
     4→ * Phase 1 only — no distributed state needed for localhost.  
     5→ */  
     6→  
     7→const limits = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>()  
     8→  
     9→const DEFAULT_MAX_ATTEMPTS = 5  
    10→const DEFAULT_WINDOW_MS = 60_000 // 1 minute  
    11→  
    12→// Note: check and record are not atomic — acceptable for Phase 1 single-process localhost.  
    13→// Phase 2: use atomic increment.  
    14→  
    15→/** Check if the rate limit allows another attempt */  
    16→export function checkRateLimit(  
    17→  key: string,  
    18→  maxAttempts: number = DEFAULT_MAX_ATTEMPTS,  
    19→  windowMs: number = DEFAULT_WINDOW_MS  
    20→): { allowed: boolean; retryAfterMs: number } {  
    21→  const now = Date.now()  
    22→  const entry = limits.get(key)  
    23→  
    24→  // Window expired — reset  
    25→  if (entry && now >= entry.resetAt) {  
    26→    limits.delete(key)  
    27→    return { allowed: true, retryAfterMs: 0 }  
    28→  }  
    29→  
    30→  // Check if over limit  
    31→  if (entry && entry.count >= maxAttempts) {  
    32→    return { allowed: false, retryAfterMs: entry.resetAt - now }  
    33→  }  
    34→  
    35→  return { allowed: true, retryAfterMs: 0 }  
    36→}  
    37→  
    38→/** Record a failed attempt */  
    39→export function recordFailure(key: string, windowMs: number = DEFAULT_WINDOW_MS): void {  
    40→  let entry = limits.get(key)  
    41→  const now = Date.now()  
    42→  // Reset expired windows so stale counts are not reused  
    43→  if (entry && now >= entry.resetAt) { entry = undefined; limits.delete(key) }  
    44→  const fresh = entry || { count: 0, resetAt: now + windowMs }  
    45→  limits.set(key, { count: fresh.count + 1, resetAt: fresh.resetAt })  
    46→}  
    47→  
    48→/** Reset rate limit on successful attempt */  
    49→export function resetRateLimit(key: string): void {  
    50→  limits.de  

... [612 more chars truncated]

     1→/**  
     2→ * Message Filter — enforces closed-team messaging isolation  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Determines whether a message from sender to recipient is allowed  
     5→ * based on governance roles (MANAGER, Chief-of-Staff) and closed-team  
     6→ * membership. Open-world agents (not in any closed team) can message  
     7→ * freely unless the recipient is inside a closed team.  
     8→ */

    21→  reason?: string

    25→ * Check whether a message from sender to recipient is allowed.  
    26→ *  
    27→ * Algorithm (R6.1–R6.7):  
    28→ * 1. Mesh-forwarded (senderAgentId null): denied if recipient is in a closed team (unverified sender)  
    29→ * 1b. Unresolved recipient (alias, not UUID) from closed-team sender: denied (prevents bypass)  
    30→ * 2. Neither in a closed team: allowed (open world, current behavior) (R6.4)  
    31→ * 3. Sender is MANAGER: always allowed (R6.3)  
    32→ * 4. Sender is COS of any closed team: can reach MANAGER, other COS, own team members (R6.2)  
    33→ * 5. Normal closed-team member: can reach same-team members and own COS (R6.1)  
    34→ * 6. Outside sender to closed-team recipient: denied (R6.5) — always reached after Steps 2–5  
    35→ *  
    36→ * IMPORTANT (R6.7): Uses getClosedTeamsForAgent (plural) to correctly handle  
    37→ * COS agents who belong to multiple closed teams simultaneously.  
    38→ */

   102→export function generateApiKey(isTest: boolean = false): string {  
   103→  const prefix = isTest ? KEY_PREFIX_TEST : KEY_PREFIX_LIVE  
   104→  const randomPart = randomBytes(KEY_LENGTH).toString('hex')  
   105→  return `${prefix}${randomPart}`  
   106→}

   114→    apiKey.length === KEY_PREFIX_LIVE.length + (KEY_LENGTH * 2)  
   115→  )  
   116→}

   198→/**  
   199→ * Extract API key from Authorization header  
   200→ * Supports "Bearer <token>" format  
   201→ */  
   202→export function extractApiKeyFromHeader(authHeader: string | null): string | null {  
   203→  if (!authHeader) return null  
   204→  
   205→  if (authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {  
   206→    return authHeader.substring(7)  
   207→  }  
   208→  
   209→  // Also accept raw key for convenience  
   210→  if (isValidApiKeyFormat(authHeader)) {  
   211→    return authHeader  
   212→  }  
   213→  
   214→  return null  
   215→}  
   216→  
   217→/**  
   218→ * Rotate an API key  
   219→ * Creates a new key and sets expiration on the old one  
   220→ */  
   221→export function rotateApiKey(oldApiKey: string): AMPKeyRotationResponse | null {  
   222→  const keys = loadApiKeys()  
   223→  const oldKeyHash = hashApiKey(oldApiKey)  
   224→  
   225→  const oldRecord = keys.find(k => k.key_hash === oldKeyHash && k.status === 'active')  
   226→  if (!oldRecord) {  
   227→    return null  
   228→  }  
   229→  
   230→  // Create new key  
   231→  const newApiKey = generateApiKey()  
   232→  const newKeyHash = hashApiKey(newApiKey)  
   233→  
   234→  const now = new Date()  
   235→  const graceExpiry = new Date(now.getTime() + KEY_ROTATION_GRACE_PERIOD_MS)  
   236→  
   237→  // Update old key with expiration  
   238→  oldRecord.expires_at = graceExpiry.toISOString()  
   239→  
   240→  // Create new key record  
   241→  const newRecord: AMPApiKeyRecord = {  
   242→    key_hash: newKeyHash,  
   243→    agent_id: oldRecord.agent_id,  
   244→    tenant_id: oldRecord.tenant_id,  
   245→    address: oldRecord.address,  
   246→    created_at: now.toISOString(),  
   247→    expires_at: null,  
   248→    status: 'active'  
   249→  }  
   250→  
   251→  keys.push(newRecord)  
   252→  saveApiKeys(keys)  
   253→  
   254→  console.log(`[AMP Auth] Rotated API key for agent ${oldRecord.agent_id.substring(0, 8)}...`)  
   255→  
   256→  return {  
   257→    api_key: newApiKey,  
   258→    expires_at: null,  
   259→    previous_key_val  

... [464 more chars truncated]

   362→ * Authenticate a request using the Authorization header  
   363→ * Returns authentication result with agent info if valid  
   364→ */  
   365→export function authenticateRequest(authHeader: string | null): AMPAuthResult {  
   366→  const apiKey = extractApiKeyFromHeader(authHeader)  
   367→  
   368→  if (!apiKey) {  
   369→    return {  
   370→      authenticated: false,  
   371→      error: 'unauthorized',  
   372→      message: 'Missing or invalid Authorization header'  
   373→    }  
   374→  }  
   375→  
   376→  const record = validateApiKey(apiKey)  
   377→  
   378→  if (!record) {  
   379→    return {  
   380→      authenticated: false,  
   381→      error: 'unauthorized',  
   382→      message: 'Invalid or expired API key'  
   383→    }  
   384→  }  
   385→  
   386→  return {  
   387→    authenticated: true,  
   388→    agentId: record.agent_id,

   391→  }

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * Agent Authentication for Internal APIs  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Bridges AMP API key auth to governance-restricted internal API calls.  
     5→ * Agents must prove identity via Bearer token for operations requiring agent identity.  
     6→ *  
     7→ * Three outcomes:  
     8→ * 1. No auth headers → system owner (web UI) → { agentId: undefined }  
     9→ * 2. Valid Authorization: Bearer → authenticated agent → { agentId: 'uuid' }  
    10→ * 3. X-Agent-Id without valid Bearer, or invalid Bearer → { error, status: 401 }  
    11→ */  
    12→import { authenticateRequest } from './amp-auth'  
    13→  
    14→export interface AgentAuthResult {  
    15→  /** Verified agent ID, or undefined for system owner / web UI */  
    16→  agentId?: string  
    17→  /** Error message if authentication failed */  
    18→  error?: string  
    19→  /** HTTP status code for the error */  
    20→  status?: number  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→/**  
    24→ * Authenticate an agent from HTTP header values.  
    25→ *  
    26→ * @param authHeader - Value of Authorization header (or null)  
    27→ * @param agentIdHeader - Value of X-Agent-Id header (or null)  
    28→ * @returns AgentAuthResult with agentId for success, error for failure, or empty for system owner  
    29→ */  
    30→export function authenticateAgent(authHeader: string | null, agentIdHeader: string | null): AgentAuthResult {  
    31→  // Case 1: No auth attempt at all → system owner / web UI  
    32→  if (!authHeader && !agentIdHeader) {  
    33→    return {}  
    34→  }  
    35→  
    36→  // Case 2: X-Agent-Id present without Authorization → reject (identity spoofing)  
    37→  if (agentIdHeader && !authHeader) {  
    38→    return {  
    39→      error: 'Agent identity requires authentication. Include Authorization: Bearer <api-key> header.',  
    40→      status: 401  
    41→    }  
    42→  }  
    43→  
    44→  // Case 3: Authorization header present → validate API key  
    45→  if (authHeader) {  
    46→    const result = authenticateRequest(authHeader)  
 

... [715 more chars truncated]  

</details>

   202→export function extractApiKeyFromHeader(authHeader: string | null): string | null {  
   203→  if (!authHeader) return null  
   204→  
   205→  if (authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {  
   206→    return authHeader.substring(7)  
   207→  }  
   208→  
   209→  // Also accept raw key for convenience  
   210→  if (isValidApiKeyFormat(authHeader)) {  
   211→    return authHeader  
   212→  }  
   213→  
   214→  return null  
   215→}  
   216→  
   217→/**  
   218→ * Rotate an API key  
   219→ * Creates a new key and sets expiration on the old one  
   220→ */  
   221→export function rotateApiKey(oldApiKey: string): AMPKeyRotationResponse | null {  
   222→  const keys = loadApiKeys()  
   223→  const oldKeyHash = hashApiKey(oldApiKey)  
   224→  
   225→  const oldRecord = keys.find(k => k.key_hash === oldKeyHash && k.status === 'active')  
   226→  if (!oldRecord) {  
   227→    return null  
   228→  }  
   229→  
   230→  // Create new key  
   231→  const newApiKey = generateApiKey()  
   232→  const newKeyHash = hashApiKey(newApiKey)  
   233→  
   234→  const now = new Date()  
   235→  const graceExpiry = new Date(now.getTime() + KEY_ROTATION_GRACE_PERIOD_MS)  
   236→  
   237→  // Update old key with expiration  
   238→  oldRecord.expires_at = graceExpiry.toISOString()  
   239→  
   240→  // Create new key record  
   241→  const newRecord: AMPApiKeyRecord = {  
   242→    key_hash: newKeyHash,  
   243→    agent_id: oldRecord.agent_id,  
   244→    tenant_id: oldRecord.tenant_id,  
   245→    address: oldRecord.address,  
   246→    created_at: now.toISOString(),  
   247→    expires_at: null,  
   248→    status: 'active'  
   249→  }  
   250→  
   251→  keys.push(newRecord)  
   252→  saveApiKeys(keys)  
   253→  
   254→  console.log(`[AMP Auth] Rotated API key for agent ${oldRecord.agent_id.substring(0, 8)}...`)  
   255→  
   256→  return {  
   257→    api_key: newApiKey,  
   258→    expires_at: null,  
   259→    previous_key_valid_until: graceExpiry.toISOString()  
   260→  }  
   261→}

   423→/**  
   424→ * Verify a message signature with the sender's public key  
   425→ */  
   426→export function verifySignature(  
   427→  message: string,  
   428→  signature: string,  
   429→  publicKeyHex: string  
   430→): boolean {  
   431→  try {  
   432→    const { verify, createPublicKey } = require('crypto')  
   433→  
   434→    // Reconstruct public key from hex  
   435→    // Ed25519 SPKI header (12 bytes) + public key (32 bytes)  
   436→    const header = Buffer.from([  
   437→      0x30, 0x2a, 0x30, 0x05, 0x06, 0x03, 0x2b, 0x65, 0x70, 0x03, 0x21, 0x00  
   438→    ])  
   439→    const publicKeyBytes = Buffer.from(publicKeyHex, 'hex')  
   440→    const spkiDer = Buffer.concat([header, publicKeyBytes])  
   441→  
   442→    const publicKey = createPublicKey({  
   443→      key: spkiDer,  
   444→      format: 'der',  
   445→      type: 'spki'  
   446→    })  
   447→  
   448→    const signatureBuffer = Buffer.from(signature, 'base64')  
   449→    return verify(null, Buffer.from(message), publicKey, signatureBuffer)  

</details>

    81→// Phase 1: No lock on read. Minor TOCTOU with setPassword(). Acceptable for single-user localhost.  
    82→// Returns false for both 'no password set' and 'wrong password'.  
    83→// Callers should check hasPassword (config.passwordHash) separately if they need to distinguish.  
    84→/** Verify plaintext against stored password hash. Returns false if no password set. */  
    85→export async function verifyPassword(plaintext: string): Promise<boolean> {  
    86→  const config = loadGovernance()  
    87→  if (!config.passwordHash) {  
    88→    // Phase 1 (localhost-only): timing difference between "no password" and "wrong password"  
    89→    // is accepted risk. No remote attackers can observe timing in this deployment model.  
    90→    return false  
    91→  }  
    92→  return bcrypt.compare(plaintext, config.passwordHash)  
    93→}
